<tr>
<td valign="top" style="width:8.51%;white-space:nowrap">
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;font-weight:bold;font-size:10pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><span style="font-weight:bold;font-size:10pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">Item&#160;2.02.</span></p></td>
<td valign="top">
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;font-weight:bold;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;"><span style="font-weight:normal;"></span>Results of Operations and Financial Condition.</p></td></tr></table></div>
<p style="margin-bottom:6pt;margin-top:6pt;text-indent:4.25%;font-size:10pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">On August 16, 2021, Annexon, Inc. (the &#8220;Company&#8221;) announced certain financial results for the second quarter ended June 30, 2021. A copy of the Company&#8217;s press release, titled &#8220;Annexon Biosciences Reports Second Quarter 2021 Financial Results and Provides Mid-Year Business Update,&#8221; is furnished pursuant to Item 2.02 as Exhibit 99.1 hereto.</p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:4.25%;font-size:10pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">The information in Item 2.02 of this Current Report on Form 8-K, including Exhibit 99.1, shall not be deemed to be &#8220;filed&#8221; for purposes of Section&#160;18 of the Securities Exchange Act of 1934, as amended, or otherwise subject to the liabilities of that section or Section&#160;11 and 12(a)(2) of the Securities Act of 1933, as amended. The information contained in Item 2.02 of this Current Report on Form 8-K, including Exhibit 99.1, shall not be incorporated by reference into any filing with the U.S. Securities and Exchange Commission (the &#8220;SEC&#8221;) made by the Company, whether made before or after the date hereof, regardless of any general incorporation language in such filing, except as expressly set forth by specific reference in such a filing.</p>
<div style="align:left;">
<table border="0" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" style="border-collapse:collapse; width:100%;">
<tr>
<td valign="top" style="width:8.51%;white-space:nowrap">
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:18pt;font-weight:bold;font-size:10pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><span style="font-weight:bold;font-size:10pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">Item&#160;</span><span style="font-weight:bold;font-size:10pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">5</span><span style="font-weight:bold;font-size:10pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">.0</span><span style="font-weight:bold;font-size:10pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">2</span><span style="font-weight:bold;font-size:10pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">.</span></p></td>
<td valign="top">
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:18pt;font-weight:bold;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;"><span style="font-weight:normal;"></span>Departure of Directors or Certain Officers&#59; Election of Directors&#59; Appointment of Certain Officers&#59; Compensatory Arrangements of Certain Officers.</p></td></tr></table></div>
<p style="margin-bottom:6pt;margin-top:6pt;text-indent:4.25%;font-size:10pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">(d) On August 12, 2021, the Board of Directors (the &#8220;Board&#8221;) of the Company appointed William D. Waddill to the Board and as chairperson of the Board&#8217;s Audit Committee (the &#8220;Audit Committee&#8221;), effectively immediately. Mr. Waddill will serve as a Class II director with a term expiring at the 2022 annual meeting of stockholders and until his successor has been elected and qualified. </p>
<p style="margin-bottom:6pt;margin-top:6pt;text-indent:4.25%;font-size:10pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">Pursuant to the Company&#8217;s non-employee director compensation program, as a non-employee director, Mr. Waddill will receive (i) a $35,000 annual retainer for his service on the Board, prorated for the remainder of 2021, (ii) a $15,000 annual retainer for his service as chairperson of the Audit Committee, prorated for the remainder of 2021, (iii) an automatic initial grant of a stock option to purchase 20,000 shares of Common Stock under the Company&#8217;s 2020 Incentive Award Plan and (iv) on the date of each annual stockholder meeting, an automatic grant of a stock option to purchase 10,000 shares of Common Stock under the Company&#8217;s 2020 Incentive Award Plan. The foregoing description is qualified in its entirety by reference to the text of the Company&#8217;s non-employee director compensation program, the form of which was filed as Exhibit 10.12 to the Company&#8217;s Registration Statement on Form S-1 filed with the SEC on July 20, 2020. </p>
<p style="margin-bottom:6pt;margin-top:6pt;text-indent:4.25%;font-size:10pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">In addition, Mr. Waddill will enter into the Company&#8217;s standard indemnification and advancement agreement for directors and executive officers, the form of which was filed as Exhibit 10.12 to the Company&#8217;s Registration Statement on Form S-1 filed with the SEC on July 2, 2020. </p>

<p style="text-align:right;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">Exhibit 99.1</p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;</p>
<div align="left">
<table border="0" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" style="border-collapse:collapse; width:21.08%;">
<tr>
<td style="width:21.08%;"></td>
</tr>
<tr style="height:35.5pt;">
<td valign="top" >
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-left:0pt;;text-indent:0pt;;color:#595959;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><img src="gz3y3ppzlbxb000001.jpg" title="" alt="" style="width:143px;height:47px;"></p></td>
</tr>
</table></div>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align:center;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-weight:bold;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">Annexon Biosciences Reports Second Quarter 2021 Financial Results and Provides Mid-Year Business Update </p>
<p style="text-align:center;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align:center;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-style:italic;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;font-weight:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#8211; Recently expanded Autoimmune franchise with advancement of third clinical candidate, ANX009, and strategically expanded into additional autoantibody-driven diseases &#8211;&nbsp;&nbsp; </p>
<p style="text-align:center;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-style:italic;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;font-weight:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#8211; Continued progress in Neurodegeneration franchise with initial Phase 2 data results from ANX005 in Huntington&#8217;s disease expected in Q4 2021 and initiation of Phase 2 ANX005 trial in Amyotrophic Lateral Sclerosis &#8211;&nbsp;&nbsp; </p>
<p style="text-align:center;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-style:italic;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;font-weight:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#8211; Appointed William D. Waddill to the Board of Directors &#8211; </p>
<p style="text-align:center;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-weight:bold;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">SOUTH SAN FRANCISCO, Calif., August 16, 2021<font style="font-weight:normal;"> &#8211; Annexon, Inc. (&#8220;Annexon&#8221;) (Nasdaq: ANNX), A</font><font style="Background-color:#FFFFFF;color:#2A3646;font-weight:normal;">nnexon, a clinical-stage biopharmaceutical company developing a class of new complement medicines for patients with classical complement-mediated autoimmune and neurodegenerative disorders of the body, brain and eye,</font><font style="font-weight:normal;"> today announced second quarter 2021 financial results and provided a mid-year business update. </font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#8220;We continue to make strong and consistent progress on our mission to deliver transformative therapies for patients suffering from classical complement-driven autoimmune and neurodegenerative diseases. With three clinical-stage drug candidates advancing in seven clinical trials, we remain laser-focused on developing game-changing therapies for patients in need while generating significant value for our shareholders,&#8221; said Douglas Love, Esq., president and chief executive officer of Annexon.&#160;&#8220;We also continue to expand our corporate capabilities and are pleased to announce the appointment of Will Waddill to our Board of Directors.&nbsp;&nbsp;Will has extensive experience in biotech and finance, and will provide an invaluable perspective as we enter our next phase of growth and value creation.&#8221;</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-weight:bold;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">Therapeutic Franchise Highlights and Updates</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">Annexon is advancing a portfolio of innovative C1 inhibitors to stop classical complement-mediated diseases at the start of the pathway in three therapeutic franchise areas:&nbsp;&nbsp;Autoimmune, Neurodegeneration and Ophthalmology.&nbsp;&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-weight:bold;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">Autoimmune Franchise</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">Annexon is pursuing a range of carefully selected neuromuscular, hematologic and nephritic antibody-mediated autoimmune indications where excess classical complement activity is a key driver of disease. During its July 28th C1q R&amp;D series presentation, Annexon showcased the rationale and potential of its anti-C1 approach in autoimmune disease.</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:8pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">Recent highlights and updates in the Autoimmune franchise include: </p>
<div align="left">
<table border="0" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0"  style="border-collapse:collapse; width:100%;">
<tr>
<td valign="top" style="width:3.33%;white-space:nowrap">
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:6pt;margin-top:0pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#auto;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;font-family:Calibri;font-size:11pt;">&nbsp;</p></td>
<td valign="top" style="width:3.33%;white-space:nowrap">
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:6pt;margin-top:0pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#auto;font-size:10pt;font-family:'Times New Roman';text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;"><font style="font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-decoration:none;Background-color:#auto;color:#auto;font-size:10pt;font-family:'Times New Roman';text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;"></font><font style="font-size:10pt;font-family:'Times New Roman'">&#8226;</font></p></td>
<td valign="top">
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:6pt;margin-top:0pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#auto;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;font-family:Calibri;font-size:11pt;"><font style="Background-color:#auto;text-decoration:none;"></font><font style="color:#000000;"></font><font style="font-weight:bold;font-size:10pt;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">Progressed enrollment in the Phase 2/3 trial of ANX005 in Guillain-Barr&#233; Syndrome (GBS), which remains on track for completion in 2023.</font><font style="font-size:10pt;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;"> Data from the completed drug-drug interaction study and Phase 1b trial were recently presented at the 2021 Peripheral Nerve Society Annual Meeting, demonstrating tolerability and full C1q target engagement of ANX005 in combination with IVIg and reduction of cerebrospinal fluid</font><font style="color:#000000;"> (</font><font style="font-size:10pt;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">CSF) complement activity following ANX005 treatment in GBS patients.</font></p></td></tr></table></div>
<div align="left">
<table border="0" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0"  style="border-collapse:collapse; width:100%;">
<tr>
<td valign="top" style="width:3.33%;white-space:nowrap">
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:6pt;margin-top:0pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#auto;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;font-family:Calibri;font-size:11pt;">&nbsp;</p></td>
<td valign="top" style="width:3.33%;white-space:nowrap">
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:6pt;margin-top:0pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#auto;font-size:10pt;font-family:'Times New Roman';text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;"><font style="font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-decoration:none;Background-color:#auto;color:#auto;font-size:10pt;font-family:'Times New Roman';text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;"></font><font style="font-size:10pt;font-family:'Times New Roman'">&#8226;</font></p></td>
<td valign="top">
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:6pt;margin-top:0pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#auto;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;font-family:Calibri;font-size:11pt;"><font style="Background-color:#auto;text-decoration:none;"></font><font style="color:#000000;"></font><font style="font-weight:bold;font-size:10pt;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">Advanced precision medicine approach to treat patients with a complement signature in the Phase 2 trial of ANX005 in warm autoimmune hemolytic anemia (wAIHA).</font><font style="font-size:10pt;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;"> In the ongoing Phase 0 (patient selection) component of the trial, several wAIHA patients have demonstrated a classical complement signature, making them potentially eligible for enrollment into the Phase 2 component of the trial. ANX005 was shown to fully inhibit complement activation of wAIHA antibodies in these patient sera. Data from the Phase 0 portion of the Phase 2 trial is expected to be submitted to a peer reviewed forum in 2021. </font></p></td></tr></table></div>
<div align="left">
<table border="0" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0"  style="border-collapse:collapse; width:100%;">
<tr>
<td valign="top" style="width:3.33%;white-space:nowrap">
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:6pt;margin-top:0pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#auto;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;font-family:Calibri;font-size:11pt;">&nbsp;</p></td>
<td valign="top" style="width:3.33%;white-space:nowrap">
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:6pt;margin-top:0pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#auto;font-size:10pt;font-family:'Times New Roman';text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;"><font style="font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-decoration:none;Background-color:#auto;color:#auto;font-size:10pt;font-family:'Times New Roman';text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;"></font><font style="font-size:10pt;font-family:'Times New Roman'">&#8226;</font></p></td>
<td valign="top">
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:6pt;margin-top:0pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#auto;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;font-family:Calibri;font-size:11pt;"><font style="Background-color:#auto;text-decoration:none;"></font><font style="color:#000000;"></font><font style="font-weight:bold;font-size:10pt;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">Strategic expansion of ANX005 into a Phase 2 program in Multifocal Motor Neuropathy (MMN), a neuromuscular disorder mechanistically related to GBS.</font><font style="font-size:10pt;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;"> Initiation of the Phase 2 study is anticipated in early 2022. </font></p></td></tr></table></div>
<div align="left">
<table border="0" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0"  style="border-collapse:collapse; width:100%;">
<tr>
<td valign="top" style="width:3.33%;white-space:nowrap">
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:6pt;margin-top:0pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#auto;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;font-family:Calibri;font-size:11pt;">&nbsp;</p></td>
<td valign="top" style="width:3.33%;white-space:nowrap">
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:6pt;margin-top:0pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#auto;font-size:10pt;font-family:'Times New Roman';text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;"><font style="font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-decoration:none;Background-color:#auto;color:#auto;font-size:10pt;font-family:'Times New Roman';text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;"></font><font style="font-size:10pt;font-family:'Times New Roman'">&#8226;</font></p></td>
<td valign="top">
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:6pt;margin-top:0pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#auto;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;font-family:Calibri;font-size:11pt;"><font style="Background-color:#auto;text-decoration:none;"></font><font style="color:#000000;"></font><font style="font-weight:bold;font-size:10pt;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">Reported Phase 1 first-in-human (FIH) data for ANX009 subcutaneous product candidate, Annexon&#8217;s third clinical stage drug candidate, which is being developed for the treatment of antibody-mediated autoimmune diseases of blood and vascular tissues.</font><font style="font-size:10pt;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;"> ANX009 was shown to be well tolerated with complete and sustained C1q inhibition, supporting twice weekly subcutaneous administration. Data from the FIH study is expected to be submitted to a peer reviewed forum in 2021.</font></p></td></tr></table></div>
<hr style="page-break-after:always;width:100%;">
<div align="left">
<table border="0" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0"  style="border-collapse:collapse; width:100%;">
<tr>
<td valign="top" style="width:3.33%;white-space:nowrap">
<p style="text-align:left;margin-bottom:6pt;margin-top:0pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#auto;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;font-family:Calibri;font-size:11pt;">&nbsp;</p></td>
<td valign="top" style="width:3.33%;white-space:nowrap">
<p style="text-align:left;margin-bottom:6pt;margin-top:0pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#auto;font-size:10pt;font-family:'Times New Roman';text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;"><font style="font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-decoration:none;Background-color:#auto;color:#auto;font-size:10pt;font-family:'Times New Roman';text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;"></font><font style="font-size:10pt;font-family:'Times New Roman'">&#8226;</font></p></td>
<td valign="top">
<p style="text-align:left;margin-bottom:6pt;margin-top:0pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#auto;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;font-family:Calibri;font-size:11pt;"><a name="_Hlk79336809"></a><font style="text-decoration:none;Background-color:#auto;font-size:10pt;font-family:'Times New Roman';"></font><font style="color:#000000;"></font><font style="font-weight:bold;font-size:10pt;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">Advanc</font><font style="font-weight:bold;font-size:10pt;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">ed</font><font style="font-weight:bold;font-size:10pt;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;"> ANX009 into a Phase 1b study in Lupus Nephritis</font><font style="font-weight:bold;font-size:10pt;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;"> (LN)</font><font style="font-weight:bold;font-size:10pt;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">, a nephritic disease characterized by autoantibody-driven activation of C1q and the classical complement pathway.</font><font style="font-size:10pt;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;"> Endogenous pathogenic anti-C1q antibodies (PACAs) have been shown to correlate with classical complement activation and disease activity. Initiation of the Phase 1b study is anticipated in early 2022 and will deploy </font><font style="font-size:10pt;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">Annexon&#8217;s</font><font style="font-size:10pt;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;"><a name="_Hlk79336809"></a> precision medicine approach targeting patients with excess classical complement and PACA activity. </font><font style="font-size:10pt;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">Complement and PACA data in LN patient samples </font><font style="font-size:10pt;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">is expected to</font><font style="font-size:10pt;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;"> be submitted to a peer reviewed forum in 2021.</font></p></td></tr></table></div>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-weight:bold;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">Neurodegeneration Franchise</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">Annexon is pioneering an approach to stop complement-mediated neurodegeneration at the start, leveraging its original discoveries of the role of C1q as a major driver of synaptic loss and neurodegeneration. Blocking C1q potentially protects against functioning synapse loss and may provide functional benefit. Annexon is utilizing biomarkers of neuronal damage to measure impact on disease. </p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:8pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">Recent highlights and updates in the Neurodegeneration franchise include: </p>
<div align="left">
<table border="0" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0"  style="border-collapse:collapse; width:100%;">
<tr>
<td valign="top" style="width:3.33%;white-space:nowrap">
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:6pt;margin-top:0pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#auto;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;font-family:Calibri;font-size:11pt;">&nbsp;</p></td>
<td valign="top" style="width:3.33%;white-space:nowrap">
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:6pt;margin-top:0pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#auto;font-size:10pt;font-family:'Times New Roman';text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;"><font style="font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-decoration:none;Background-color:#auto;color:#auto;font-size:10pt;font-family:'Times New Roman';text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;"></font><font style="font-size:10pt;font-family:'Times New Roman'">&#8226;</font></p></td>
<td valign="top">
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:6pt;margin-top:0pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#auto;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;font-family:Calibri;font-size:11pt;"><font style="Background-color:#auto;text-decoration:none;"></font><font style="color:#000000;"></font><font style="font-weight:bold;font-size:10pt;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">Completed enrollment in Phase 2 trial of ANX005 in Huntington&#8217;s Disease (HD) and expects to report initial data in Q4 2021. </font></p></td></tr></table></div>
<div align="left">
<table border="0" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0"  style="border-collapse:collapse; width:100%;">
<tr>
<td valign="top" style="width:3.33%;white-space:nowrap">
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:6pt;margin-top:0pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#auto;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;font-family:Calibri;font-size:11pt;">&nbsp;</p></td>
<td valign="top" style="width:3.33%;white-space:nowrap">
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:6pt;margin-top:0pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#auto;font-size:10pt;font-family:'Times New Roman';text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;"><font style="font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-decoration:none;Background-color:#auto;color:#auto;font-size:10pt;font-family:'Times New Roman';text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;"></font><font style="font-size:10pt;font-family:'Times New Roman'">&#8226;</font></p></td>
<td valign="top">
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:6pt;margin-top:0pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#auto;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;font-family:Calibri;font-size:11pt;"><font style="Background-color:#auto;text-decoration:none;"></font><font style="color:#000000;"></font><font style="font-weight:bold;font-size:10pt;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">Initiated patient dosing in Phase 2 trial of ANX005 in Amyotrophic Lateral Sclerosis (ALS) and now expects to report data in 2022 due to slower initial enrollment. </font></p></td></tr></table></div>
<div align="left">
<table border="0" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0"  style="border-collapse:collapse; width:100%;">
<tr>
<td valign="top" style="width:3.33%;white-space:nowrap">
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:6pt;margin-top:0pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#auto;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;font-family:Calibri;font-size:11pt;">&nbsp;</p></td>
<td valign="top" style="width:3.33%;white-space:nowrap">
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:6pt;margin-top:0pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#auto;font-size:10pt;font-family:'Times New Roman';text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;"><font style="font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-decoration:none;Background-color:#auto;color:#auto;font-size:10pt;font-family:'Times New Roman';text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;"></font><font style="font-size:10pt;font-family:'Times New Roman'">&#8226;</font></p></td>
<td valign="top">
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:6pt;margin-top:0pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#auto;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;font-family:Calibri;font-size:11pt;"><font style="Background-color:#auto;text-decoration:none;"></font><font style="color:#000000;"></font><font style="font-weight:bold;font-size:10pt;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">Completed preclinical study of ANX005 in SOD1 model of ALS, which demonstrated preserved neuromuscular function and reduced neuronal damage as measured by Neurofilament Light Chain (NfL).</font><font style="font-size:10pt;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;"> </font><font style="Background-color:#FFFFFF;color:#2A3646;font-size:10pt;font-family:Times New Roman;">Data from the SOD1 preclinical study represent the third instance of NfL reduction by ANX005, following the Phase 1b trial in GBS patients and R6/2 preclinical model of HD. Results from the ALS preclinical study are expected to be submitted to a peer-reviewed forum in 2021.&#160;</font></p></td></tr></table></div>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-weight:bold;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">Ophthalmology Franchise</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:8pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">Annexon is utilizing intravitreal administration of ANX007 to inhibit C1q, which is implicated in neurodegeneration in the retina. Selectively targeting C1q at the start of the classical pathway versus downstream approaches may enhance efficacy and safety for patients in ophthalmic disorders, including Geographic Atrophy (GA)<font style="font-size:11pt;font-family:Calibri;">.&nbsp;&nbsp;</font><font style="font-weight:bold;font-size:11pt;font-family:Calibri;"> </font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:8pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">Recent highlights and updates in the Ophthalmology franchise include: </p>

<td valign="top" style="width:3.33%;white-space:nowrap">

<p style="text-align:left;Background-color:#FFFFFF;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#auto;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;"><font style="Background-color:#auto;text-decoration:none;"></font><font style="color:#000000;"></font><font style="font-weight:bold;color:#000000;">Net loss:</font><font style="color:#000000;"> Net loss was $31.3 million for the quarter ended June 30, 2021, and $57.4 million for the six months ended June 30, 2021, compared to $12.2 million for the quarter ended June 31, 2020, and $24.6 million for the six months ended June 30, 2020. </font><font style="color:#000000;">Net loss attributable to common stockholders was $31.3 million or $0.82 per share for the quarter ended June 30, 2021, and $57.4 million or $1.50 per share for the </font><font style="color:#000000;">six months</font><font style="color:#000000;"> ended June 30, 2021, compared to $12.5 million or $28.87 per share for the quarter ended June 30, 2020, and $25.1 million or $57.96 per share for the </font><font style="color:#000000;">six months</font><font style="color:#000000;"> ended June 30, 2020. </font></p></td></tr></table></div>
<p style="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-weight:bold;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">About Annexon, Inc.</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;Background-color:#FFFFFF;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:6pt;text-indent:0%;font-size:10pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">Annexon is a clinical-stage biopharmaceutical company developing a class of new complement medicines for patients with classical complement-mediated disorders of the body, brain and eye. The company&#8217;s pipeline is based on its platform technology addressing a broad spectrum of well-researched classical complement-mediated autoimmune and neurodegenerative diseases triggered by aberrant activation of C1q, the initiating molecule of the classical complement pathway. Annexon is advancing a portfolio of innovative product candidates designed to block the activity of C1q and the entire classical complement pathway:&nbsp;&nbsp;ANX005 (intravenous administration), ANX007 (intravitreal administration), and ANX009 (subcutaneous administration). Annexon is deploying a disciplined, biomarker-driven strategy designed to improve the probability of technical success of its portfolio. For more information, visit <font style="text-decoration:underline;">www.annexonbio.com</font>.</p>
<p style="Background-color:#FFFFFF;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;">&nbsp;</p>
